<body link="blue" vlink="purple">

<div style="font-family:'Times New Roman';">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.1</font></b></p>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></address>

<kbd style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple Reports Third Quarter Results</font></kbd>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Revenue Increases 30 Percent and Net Profit Triples
Year-Over-Year</font></address>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">CUPERTINO, California&#151;July 14, 2004&#151;Apple&#174; today
announced financial results for its fiscal 2004 third quarter ended June 26,
2004. For the quarter, the Company posted a net profit of $61 million, or $.16
per diluted share. These results compare to a net profit of $19 million, or
$.05 per diluted share, in the year-ago quarter. Revenue for the quarter was
$2.014 billion, up 30 percent from the year-ago quarter. Gross margin was 27.8
percent, up from 27.7 percent in the year-ago quarter. International sales
accounted for 39 percent of the quarter&#146;s revenue. </font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The quarter&#146;s results include an after-tax
restructuring charge of $6 million. Excluding this charge, the Company&#146;s net
profit for the quarter would have been $67 million, or $.17 per diluted share. </font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple shipped 876 thousand Macintosh&#174; units and 860
thousand iPods during the quarter, representing a 14 percent increase in CPU
units and a 183 percent increase in iPods over the year-ago quarter.</font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;It was an outstanding quarter&#151;our highest third
quarter revenue in eight years,&#148; said Steve Jobs, Apple&#146;s CEO. &#147;Our Mac-based
revenue grew a healthy 19 percent, and our music-based revenue grew an
incredible 162 percent. We&#146;ve got a strong product portfolio, with some amazing
new additions coming later this year.&#148;</font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We were very pleased with our 30 percent
year-over-year revenue growth and our operating margin expansion,&#148; said Peter
Oppenheimer, Apple&#146;s CFO. &#147;Looking ahead to the fourth quarter of fiscal 2004,
we expect revenue of about $2.1 billion and earnings per diluted share of $.16
to $.17, including $.01 per diluted share in restructuring charges.&#148;</font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Non-GAAP Measures</font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company believes that presentation of results
excluding items such as restructuring charges and investment gains provides
meaningful supplemental information to both management and investors that is
indicative of the Company&#146;s core operating results and facilitates comparison
of operating results across reporting periods.</font></address>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>


<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\jms\spadi\04-7804-1\task147293\7804-1-mm.htm',USER='vgram',CD='Jul 14 06:05 2004' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
</font>

<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">&nbsp;</p>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple will provide live streaming of its Q3 2004
financial results conference call utilizing QuickTime&#153;, Apple&#146;s standards-based
technology for live and on-demand audio and video streaming. The live webcast
will begin at 2:00 p.m. PDT on Wednesday, July 14, 2004 at
http://www.apple.com/quicktime/qtv/earningsq304/ and will also be available for
replay. The QuickTime player is available free for Macintosh and Windows users
at www.apple.com/quicktime.</font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press release contains forward-looking statements
about the Company&#146;s estimated revenue and earnings for the fourth quarter of
fiscal 2004. These statements involve risks and uncertainties and actual
results may differ. Potential risks and uncertainties include continued
competitive pressures in the marketplace; the effect competitive and economic
factors and the Company&#146;s reaction to them may have on consumer and business
buying decisions with respect to the Company&#146;s products; the ability of the
Company to make timely delivery of new programs, products and successful
technological innovations to the marketplace; the continued availability of
certain components and services essential to the Company&#146;s business currently
obtained by the Company from sole or limited sources, including the timely
resolution of manufacturing issues associated with the G5 microprocessors used
in many of the Company&#146;s Macintosh systems; possible disruption in commercial
activities caused by terrorist activity and armed conflict, such as changes in
logistics and security arrangements, and reduced end-user purchases relative to
expectations; possible disruption in commercial activity as a result of major
health concerns, such as Severe Acute Respiratory Syndrome (SARS); risks associated
with the Company&#146;s retail initiative including significant investment cost,
uncertain consumer acceptance and potential impact on existing reseller
relationships; the effect that the Company&#146;s dependency on manufacturing and
logistics services provided by third-parties may have on the quality or
quantity of products manufactured; the Company&#146;s reliance on the availability
of third-party music content, and the ability of the Company to successfully
evolve its operating system and attract sufficient Macintosh developers. More
information on potential factors that could affect the Company&#146;s financial
results is included from time to time in the Company&#146;s public reports filed
with the SEC, including the Company&#146;s Form 10-K for the fiscal year 2003; the
Company&#146;s Forms 10-Q for the quarters ended December 27, 2003 and March 27,
2004; and the Company&#146;s Form 10-Q for the quarter ended June 26, 2004 to be
filed with the SEC. The Company assumes no obligation to update any
forward-looking statements or information, which speak as of their respective
dates.</font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></address>

<address style="font-style:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple ignited the personal computer revolution in the
1970s with the Apple II and reinvented the personal computer in the 1980s with
the Macintosh. Today, Apple continues to lead the industry in innovation with its
award-winning desktop and notebook computers, OS X operating system, and iLife
and professional applications. Apple is also spearheading the digital music
revolution with its iPod portable music players and iTunes online music store.</font></address>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
